function MSGVerticalMultiMenu(id, bIsIE7) {
    this.sMainTableId = id;
    this.sCurrentOpenSubMenu = '';
    this.sDirection = 'ltr';
    this.bIsIE7 = bIsIE7;

    this.initsubMenus = function(sDistance) {
        var oMainTable = document.getElementById('ul_' + this.sMainTableId);
        this.sDirection = $(oMainTable).css('direction');
        if (!this.sDirection) {
            this.sDirection = 'ltr';
        }
        if (sDistance && oMainTable) {
           if ((sDistance.length > 2) && (sDistance.indexOf('px') == -1)) {
               sDistance += 'px';
           }
           elementList = oMainTable.getElementsByTagName('ul');
           if (elementList) {
               for (var i = 0; i < elementList.length; i++) {
                   var element = elementList[i];
                   if (this.sDirection == 'ltr') {
                       element.style.left = sDistance;
                   } else {
                       element.style.right = sDistance;
                   }
               }
           }
        } else if (oMainTable) {
            this.initDefaultPositions($(oMainTable));
            oMainTable.className = oMainTable.className;
       } 
    }; 

    this.showSubMenuById = function(sId) {
       var sOpenSub = this.oCurrentOpenSubMenu;
       if (sOpenSub) {
           this.hideSubMenuById(sOpenSub);
       }
       if (sOpenSub != sId) {
           var oSubMenu = document.getElementById('ul_' + sId);
           if (oSubMenu) {
               var aMenuItem = document.getElementById('li_' + sId);
               oSubMenu.style.display = 'block';
               this.oCurrentOpenSubMenu = sId;
           }
       }
       return false;
    }; 

    this.hideSubMenuById = function(sId) {
       var oSubMenu = document.getElementById('ul_' + sId);
       if (oSubMenu) {
           oSubMenu.style.display = 'none';
           this.oCurrentOpenSubMenu = '';
       }
       return false;
    };

    this.onMouseOver = function(oItem) {        
        if (this.oItemToHide && this.oItemToHide != oItem) {            
            this.oItemToHide.className = '';
        }
        
        if (oItem.timeout) {
            clearTimeout(oItem.timeout);
        }
                
        oItem.className = 'li_hover';                
    };

    this.onMouseOut = function(oItem) {
        oItem.timeout = setTimeout(function() {            
            oItem.className = '';
        }, 400);
        this.oItemToHide = oItem;
    };

    this.initDefaultPositions = function(oUL) {
        var that = this;
        if (oUL) {
            var jPos = oUL.position();
            var iWidth = oUL.width();
            var aSubULs = oUL.find('li>ul');
            if (aSubULs && aSubULs.length > 0) {
                var x;
                for (var i = 0; i< aSubULs.length; i++) {
                    var oSubUL = $(aSubULs[i]);
                    var sPosType = that.sDirection == 'rtl' ? 'right' : 'left';
                    oSubUL.css(sPosType, jPos.left + iWidth + 'px');
                    if (that.bIsIE7) {
                        var sAlterPosType = that.sDirection == 'rtl' ? 'left' : 'right';
                        oSubUL.css(sAlterPosType, '0px');
                    }
                    that.initDefaultPositions(oSubUL);
                }
            }
        }
    };

};
function msginitc_inc37_menu_menucomp1() {
tmmenu_inc37_menu_menucomp1 = new MSGTabsMultiMenu('inc37_menu_menucomp1', false, false, 0); tmmenu_inc37_menu_menucomp1.init();
};

};
